# AKTI Spark lower_snake_case Path Migration Plan v1

Status: AKTI_UNDERSCORE_PATH_MIGRATION_PLAN_READY_FOR_REVIEW

## Purpose

This document plans AKTI Spark's migration toward lower_snake_case paths and industry-aware domain/version organization. It is planning/control only. It does not rename files, move files, modify imports, modify routes, modify APIs, modify package or lockfile files, modify Prisma/schema/migrations/generated registry, start Phase 6, deploy, or access secrets.

Spark Genesis now uses lower_snake_case path policy. AKTI Spark should align over time without breaking routes, imports, audit history, source-of-truth references, or historical evidence truthfulness.

## Current Main HEAD

`07bd43b1f4abfb1c3cdf6320c2bbd2f2977c4665`

Phase 5C merge commit `501843766e235fec6a5062678e07fada85ef33ca` is reachable from this head.

## Inventory Summary

Inventory was generated from tracked files with these read-only commands:

```bash
git ls-files | awk '{ if ($0 ~ /-/) print }' | sort
git ls-files | awk -F/ '{base=$NF; if (base ~ /-/) print}' | sort
git ls-files | awk -F/ '{for(i=1;i<=NF;i++){if($i ~ /-/) print $0}}' | sort -u
rg -n "lead-desk|phase5|phase-5|codex-review|ticket-pack|seed-matrix|spark-genesis|display-features|module-registry|access-core|gatekeeper|audit-report|final-external-audit|final-screenshots" .
```

Summary:

| Metric | Count |
| --- | ---: |
| Tracked paths containing any hyphen | 1462 |
| Tracked paths with hyphenated basename | 1425 |
| Tracked paths with any hyphenated segment | 1462 |
| Reference-search file hits | 285 |

Classification summary:

| Category | Count |
| --- | ---: |
| A - Docs/path-policy/index candidates | 34 |
| B - Internal code/import candidates | 160 |
| C - Route/API/public-surface candidates | 91 |
| D - Package/tool convention paths | 3 |
| E - Historical audit/evidence references | 1174 |
| Total classified hyphenated tracked paths | 1462 |

## Classification Rules

| Category | Meaning | Default handling |
| --- | --- | --- |
| A - Docs/path-policy/index candidate | Docs, planning/control, ADR, screen-contract, or process paths that can usually be indexed, copied, or migrated after reference review. | Prefer index/copy first. Move only after references, source-of-truth rank, and historical links are preserved. |
| B - Internal code/import candidate | Internal helper, component, test, script, package, or library paths without direct route/API semantics. | Requires import/reference updates and validation in a dedicated internal filename migration PR. |
| C - Route/API/public-surface candidate | Paths that may affect URLs, API modules, controller/module boundaries, route contracts, manifests, or CRM/Lead Desk compatibility. | Do not rename without compatibility plan, redirects or aliases if needed, screen/API contract updates, screenshots, and human approval. |
| D - Package/tool convention path | Paths controlled by tools, frameworks, lockfiles, CI, or external conventions. | Leave unchanged unless a tool-convention migration explicitly approves a change. |
| E - Historical audit/evidence reference | Existing audit packages, screenshot manifests, commit logs, ticket artifacts, and evidence paths. | Preserve historical truth. Prefer new indexed/copy structures over rewriting old evidence. |

## Target Path Policy

Use lower_snake_case for new AKTI-generated directories and filenames.

Rules:

- Use underscores, not hyphens, in new AKTI-generated paths unless an external framework or explicit migration exception requires a hyphen.
- Use version folders such as `v0_0_1`.
- Use phase folders such as `phase_05c`.
- Use singular industry names, including `training`, not `trainings`.
- Do not rewrite historical artifact paths in place.
- Do not rename Route/API/public-surface paths without compatibility proof and human approval.

Correct examples:

```text
docs/process/core/v0_0_1/phase_05c/
codex-review/core/v0_0_1/phase_05c/final_external_audit/
apps/training/crm/v0_0_1/
apps/training/hr/v0_0_1/
apps/training/finance/v0_0_1/
apps/healthcare/patient_management/v0_0_1/
apps/fmcg/distribution/v0_0_1/
```

## Core v0.0.1 Baseline Decision

Core `v0_0_1` means the completed platform/core baseline through Phase 5C, including Phase 1 through Phase 5C control docs, execution evidence, validation evidence, and final audit artifacts.

Core `v0_0_1` should be indexed before moving or copying artifacts. Historical locations remain truthful and must not be silently rewritten.

## Core v0.0.2 Next-Update Decision

The next Core update should use `core/v0_0_2` unless a major architecture change justifies `core/v0_1_0` with explicit human approval and supporting architecture rationale.

This migration plan itself lives under `docs/process/core/v0_0_2/` because it plans the next organization update after the Core `v0_0_1` baseline.

## Industry-Aware App Path Policy

Future app/domain paths should be industry-aware and versioned:

```text
apps/training/crm/v0_0_1
apps/training/hr/v0_0_1
apps/training/finance/v0_0_1
apps/healthcare/patient_management/v0_0_1
apps/fmcg/distribution/v0_0_1
```

Rules:

- Use `training`, not `trainings`.
- Use lower_snake_case for multi-word domains, for example `patient_management`.
- Do not create Phase 6 modules from this migration plan.
- Do not create future app/domain paths until their domain truth docs, contracts, manifests, and approval gates exist.

## Migration PR Train

### PR 1 - Path Policy and Indexes Only

Create only index and policy files such as:

- `docs/process/index.md`
- `docs/process/core/v0_0_1/index.md`
- `codex-review/core/v0_0_1/index.md`

Purpose: map legacy Phase 0-5C artifacts into Core `v0_0_1` without moving files.

### PR 2 - docs/process Copy-or-Move Plan

Plan and then execute either copy, move, or alias behavior for docs into:

```text
docs/process/core/v0_0_1/phase_*/
```

Historical links must remain valid or be indexed with clear provenance.

### PR 3 - codex-review Migration Plan

Plan and then execute either copy, move, or alias behavior for evidence artifacts into:

```text
codex-review/core/v0_0_1/phase_*/
```

Final audit and screenshot references must remain truthful. Existing evidence should not be rewritten in place.

### PR 4 - Internal Code Filename Migration

Only after inventory review confirms safe internal candidates. This PR may rename internal helper, component, library, or test filenames and update imports/references.

Validation must include the relevant targeted tests plus full lint/typecheck/test/build as needed.

### PR 5 - Route/API Public-Surface Migration Plan

Only if the team decides to rename public route/API paths. This is not a docs-only migration.

Requirements:

- compatibility plan;
- redirects or aliases where required;
- route contracts;
- API contracts;
- module manifest updates if affected;
- screenshot coverage;
- human approval.

Do not merge Route/API renames into docs-only migration PRs.

## Files and Paths That Must Not Be Renamed Yet

Do not rename these path families in the initial migration PRs:

- `apps/web/app/lead-desk/**`
- `apps/api/src/lead-desk/**`
- `apps/api/src/access-core/**`
- `apps/api/src/module-registry/**`
- `apps/api/src/data-controls/**`
- `apps/api/src/platform-health/**`
- `apps/api/src/file-service/**`
- `apps/api/src/engagement-gateway/**`
- `codex-review/**` historical evidence paths, unless copied or indexed with provenance
- `.github/workflows/**` unless CI/tooling migration is explicitly approved
- `pnpm-lock.yaml`
- `apps/web/next-env.d.ts`

## Route/API Compatibility Risks

Route/API path changes can affect:

- user-facing URLs;
- Next.js app route resolution;
- NestJS controller/module imports;
- contracts and module manifests;
- tests and screenshots;
- audit references;
- CRM visible-label-over-Lead-Desk compatibility;
- existing external bookmarks or scripts.

Route/API migrations require a separate compatibility design, explicit human approval, and validation beyond this docs/control plan.

## Validation Ladder for Future Migration PRs

Docs/index PRs:

```bash
rg "core/v0_0_1" docs/process codex-review
rg "phase_05c" docs/process codex-review
git diff --check
git status --short --branch
```

Docs/codex-review copy or move PRs:

```bash
rg "legacy" docs/process codex-review
rg "artifact_manifest" codex-review
git diff --check
git status --short --branch
```

Internal code filename PRs:

```bash
pnpm lint
pnpm typecheck
pnpm test
pnpm build
git diff --check
git status --short --branch
```

Contract or manifest-impacting PRs, if separately approved:

```bash
pnpm contracts:validate
pnpm lint
pnpm typecheck
pnpm test
pnpm build
git diff --check
git status --short --branch
```

Route/API migration PRs, if separately approved:

```bash
pnpm contracts:validate
pnpm lint
pnpm typecheck
pnpm test
pnpm build
# plus route/API compatibility tests and screenshot validation defined by the approved migration plan
git diff --check
git status --short --branch
```

## Human Approval Triggers

Human approval is required before:

- renaming Route/API/public-surface paths;
- changing `lead-desk` technical routes, files, APIs, contracts, models, or manifests;
- changing package, lockfile, CI, or framework-convention paths;
- moving ADRs or source-of-truth docs;
- rewriting historical evidence paths;
- changing Prisma/schema/migrations/generated registry;
- changing public package entrypoints;
- creating Phase 6 plans, tickets, or modules;
- changing deployment, auth, secrets, or production configuration.

## Recommended Next Step

Create PR 1: path policy and indexes only.

Recommended files for PR 1:

- `docs/process/index.md`
- `docs/process/core/v0_0_1/index.md`
- `codex-review/core/v0_0_1/index.md`

PR 1 should not move any legacy file. It should introduce the Core `v0_0_1` index and map legacy Phase 0-5C artifacts to their current locations.
